import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    latest_start: int = float('inf')
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int, num_operations: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.num_operations = num_operations
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

def create_jssp_instance(job_data):
    """Create JSSP instance from parsed job data"""
    
    instance = JSSSPInstance(num_jobs=40, num_machines=20)
    
    # Add operations with precedence constraints
    for job_id, operations in job_data.items():
        for op_id, (machine_id, processing_time) in enumerate(operations):
            # Add precedence constraint from previous operation in same job
            predecessors = []
            if op_id > 0:
                predecessors.append((job_id, op_id - 1))
            
            instance.add_operation(job_id, op_id, machine_id, processing_time, predecessors)
    
    return instance

def priority_list_scheduling(instance: JSSSPInstance):

import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    latest_start: int = float('inf')
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int, num_operations: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.num_operations = num_operations
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

def create_jssp_instance(job_data):
    """Create JSSP instance from parsed job data"""
    
    instance = JSSSPInstance(num_jobs=40, num_machines=20)
    
    # Add operations with precedence constraints
    for job_id, operations in job_data.items():
        for op_id, (machine_id, processing_time) in enumerate(operations):
            # Add precedence constraint from previous operation in same job
            predecessors = []
            if op_id > 0:
                predecessors.append((job_id, op_id - 1))
            
            instance.add_operation(job_id, op_id, machine_id, processing_time, predecessors)
    
    return instance

import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    latest_start: int = float('inf')
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int, num_operations: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.num_operations = num_operations
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import heapq
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict, Set

@dataclass
class Operation:
    job_id: int
    op_id: int
    machine_id: int
    processing_time: int
    predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    successors: List[Tuple[int, int]]
    earliest_start: int = 0
    scheduled_start: int = -1
    scheduled_end: int = -1

class JSSSPInstance:
    def __init__(self, num_jobs: int, num_machines: int):
        self.num_jobs = num_jobs
        self.num_machines = num_machines
        self.operations = {}
        self.machine_operations = defaultdict(list)
        self.job_operations = defaultdict(list)
        
    def add_operation(self, job_id: int, op_id: int, machine_id: int, 
                     processing_time: int, predecessors: List[Tuple[int, int]] = None):
        if predecessors is None:
            predecessors = []
            
        op = Operation(
            job_id=job_id,
            op_id=op_id,
            machine_id=machine_id,
            processing_time=processing_time,
            predecessors=predecessors,
            successors=[]
        )
        
        self.operations[(job_id, op_id)] = op
        self.machine_operations[machine_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        self.job_operations[job_id].append((job_id, op_id))
        
        # Build successor relationships
        for pred_job, pred_op in predecessors:
            if (pred_job, pred_op) in self.operations:
                self.operations[(pred_job, pred_op)].successors.append((job_id, op_id))

def create_jssp_instance(job_data):
    """Create JSSP instance from parsed job data"""
    
    instance = JSSSPInstance(num_jobs=40, num_machines=20)
    
    # Add operations with precedence constraints
    for job_id, operations in job_data.items():
        for op_id, (machine_id, processing_time) in enumerate(operations):
            # Add precedence constraint from previous operation in same job
            predecessors = []
            if op_id > 0:
                predecessors.append((job_id, op_id - 1))
            
            instance.add_operation(job_id, op_id, machine_id, processing_time, predecessors)
    
    return instance
